Connecting w/the Community	At town halls &amp; community events, I enjoy listening &amp; learning about what's important to families, neighbors, and friends. From Culpeper to Nottoway, I will be a representative who is accountable, and provides a voice, to all residents of the 7th. #VA07
Climate Change	The science is real &amp; I believe climate change is a threat to our economy &amp; national security. Congress should lead the way fighting climate change by researching &amp; investing in renewable energy; huge opportunity to grow this sector &amp; create well-paying jobs.
Higher Education	All students should have access to education &amp; not leave school with massive debt. I will work to make 2&amp;4 year colleges more affordable, increase access to federal grants &amp; loanrepayment/forgiveness opportunities, &amp; strengthen vocational/apprenticeship programs.
Gun Violence Prevention	As a former law enforcement officer, I am comfortable around guns, but believe we must stop gun violence and save lives. I support universal background checks, Extreme Risk Protective Orders, banning bump stocks, and reenacting the assault weapons ban.
Farm Bill	We absolutely need to fully fund, and ensure that SNAP is funded so that we can support those who are most vulnerable and help lift them out of poverty.
Infrastructure Funding	I believe investing in infrastructure is crucial for public safety and economic development. We need to make across the board infrastructure investments, and adopt a long term vision so that our country continues to grow and prosper.
Jobs in Rural VA	High speed broadband, investment in educational training, affordable childcare, and access to healthcare are crucial to attracting jobs &amp; businesses in rural areas, and as a member of Congress, I will ensure that we support and strengthen our rural workers.
Rising Cost of Healthcare	Health insurance should be affordable &amp; accessible for all families. I support Medicare X: lowers cost of coverage by allowing people to buy into Medicare. Combat rising drug prices: I would work to allow Medicare to negotiate directly w/drug companies.
Enhancing #Healthcare in Rural Areas	I believe all Americans should have accessible &amp; affordable healthcare. I support the Save Our Rural Hospitals Act, &amp; would work to increase funding for ambulances, hospitals, &amp; preventative care in rural areas.
What excites you about south side VA?	I am excited to meet neighbors &amp; learn the different needs of our diverse district. I have a strong desire to know all communities, and work to represent their best interests as a member of Congress.
